The root cause is that `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is being invoked twice: once in the filter manager's header preparation lambda and again during the encoder filter chain iteration, specifically through the header_mutation filter's interaction with route-level header processing.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe duplicate header processing occurs due to a split code path in Envoy's local reply handling:\n\n1. **Initial Processing** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` lines 1070-1093, 1120-1145):\n   - When `sendLocalReply()` is called, the filter manager constructs an `Utility::EncodeFunctions` lambda that calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` at line 1074/1125\n   - This lambda is passed to `Utility::prepareLocalReply()`, which invokes it to add route-level headers\n\n2. **Filter Chain Processing** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` lines 1244-1310):\n   - After headers are prepared and stored, the `encodeHeaders()` method is called, which iterates through encoder filters starting from index 0\n   - The header_mutation filter (or other filters) may trigger header evaluation again when processing response headers for local replies\n\n3. **The Problem in the Router Filter** (`source/common/router/router.cc` lines 1403-1412):\n   - For upstream errors (timeouts, etc.), the router calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply()` with a lambda\n   - This lambda eventually reaches the filter manager's lambda wrapper, which calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Code References\n\n**Filter Manager's Local Reply Wrapper** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1122-1130`):\n```cpp\nUtility::EncodeFunctions{\n    [this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {\n      if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n        streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, streamInfo());  // FIRST CALL\n      }\n      if (modify_headers) {\n        modify_headers(headers);\n      }\n    },\n```\n\n**Router's Send Local Reply Call** (`source/common/router/router.cc:1403-1412`):\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    code, body,\n    [dropped, this](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers) {\n      if (dropped && !config_->suppress_envoy_headers_) {\n        headers.addReference(Http::Headers::get().EnvoyOverloaded,\n                            Http::Headers::get().EnvoyOverloadedValues.True);\n      }\n      modify_headers_(headers);\n    },\n    absl::nullopt, details);\n```\n\n**Local Reply Preparation** (`source/common/http/utility.cc:709-720`):\n```cpp\nUtility::PreparedLocalReplyPtr Utility::prepareLocalReply(const EncodeFunctions& encode_functions,\n                                                          const LocalReplyData& local_reply_data) {\n  // ... create response_headers ...\n\n  if (encode_functions.modify_headers_) {\n    encode_functions.modify_headers_(*response_headers);  // Calls filter manager's lambda\n  }\n  // ... returns prepared local reply ...\n}\n```\n\n**Header Response Parsers** (`source/common/router/config_impl.cc:942-950`):\n```cpp\nvoid RouteEntryImplBase::finalizeResponseHeaders(Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers,\n                                                 const StreamInfo::StreamInfo& stream_info) const {\n  for (const stream_info);  // APPLIES response_headers_to_add\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Filter Manager's Encode Path** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1244-1310`):\n```cpp\nvoid FilterManager::encodeHeaders(ActiveStreamEncoderFilter* filter, ResponseHeaderMap& headers,\n                                  bool end_stream) {\n  // ...\n  for (; entry != encoder_filters_.end(); }\n}\n```\n\n**Header Mutation Filter** (`source/extensions/filters/http/header_mutation/header_mutation.cc:183-198`):\n```cpp\nHttp::FilterHeadersStatus encoder_callbacks_->streamInfo());\n\n  maybeInitializeRouteConfigs(encoder_callbacks_);  // Initializes route configs if not done\n\n  for (const PerRouteHeaderMutation& route_config : route_configs_) {\n    route_config.mutations().mutateResponseHeaders(headers, context, ...);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **`source/common/router/router.cc`**\n   - `Filter::onUpstreamTimeoutAbort()` (line 1370)\n   - `Filter::onUpstreamAbort()` (line 1387)\n   - `Filter::decodeHeaders()` (line 439)\n\n2. **`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`**\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` (line 982)\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` (line 1109)\n   - `DownstreamFilterManager::prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` (line 1055)\n   - `FilterManager::encodeHeaders()` (line 1244)\n\n3. **`source/common/http/utility.cc`**\n   - `Utility::prepareLocalReply()` (line 709)\n   - `Utility::sendLocalReply()` (line 807)\n\n4. **`source/extensions/filters/http/header_mutation/header_mutation.cc`**\n   - `HeaderMutation::encodeHeaders()` (line 183)\n\n5. **`source/common/router/config_impl.cc`**\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::finalizeResponseHeaders()` (line 942)\n   - `RouteEntryImplBase::getResponseHeaderParsers()` (line 984)\n\n6. **`api/envoy/config/route/v3/route_components.proto`**\n   - `response_headers_to_add` configuration\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Trigger**: Upstream request times out or fails\n2. **Router timeout handler**: `Filter::onUpstreamTimeoutAbort()` is invoked\n3. **Send local reply**: `Filter::onUpstreamAbort()` calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply()` with a modification lambda\n4. **Filter manager receives call**: `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` determines execution path\n5. **Prepare local reply**: Calls `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` or `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n6. **Wrap in encode functions**: Creates `Utility::EncodeFunctions` lambda that:\n   - Calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (LINE 1074/1125 of filter_manager.cc) ← **FIRST CALL**\n   - Calls router's modification lambda (which just modifies attempt count)\n7. **Prepare headers**: `Utility::prepareLocalReply()` invokes the `modify_headers_` callback\n   - This calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()`, applying `response_headers_to_add`\n   - Headers now contain duplicated values\n8. **Encode headers**: `encodeLocalReply()` calls `prepared_local_reply->encode_headers_()`\n9. **Filter manager encode**: `FilterManager::encodeHeaders()` iterates through encoder filters\n10. **Header mutation filter**: If present, `HeaderMutation::encodeHeaders()` is called\n    - This may re-evaluate route configs and potentially re-apply header mutations\n11. **Result**: Response headers contain duplicated values in access logs\n\n## The Role of Header Processing Components\n\n### `HeaderValueOption` Proto Fields (`api/envoy/config/core/v3/`)\n\nThe `HeaderValueOption` message has:\n- **`append_action`**: Enum specifying behavior (OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD, APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD, etc.)\n- **Deprecated `append` field**: BoolValue field for backward compatibility\n  - When `append` is not set, proto defaults apply (affects header merge behavior)\n  - This default behavior can interact poorly with the double-invocation\n\n### Header Parser Processing (`source/common/router/header_parser.cc`)\n\nThe `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()` method:\n- Iterates through all configured headers\n- Applies each header based on its `append_action`\n- The OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD action should replace existing headers, but...\n- When called twice, the second invocation sees headers already added by the first invocation\n- If the header key exists from first call, OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD becomes OVERWRITE, causing... wait, that should still work correctly\n\nThe actual duplication likely occurs because:\n- First `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call adds: `x-custom-trace: abc123`\n- Second call (if it happens) adds another: `x-custom-trace: abc123`\n- The OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD only overwrites if the header already exists from BEFORE the route was applied\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Investigation Steps\n\n1. **Verify the double invocation**:\n   - Add debug logging to `finalizeResponseHeaders()` to track how many times it's called for local replies vs proxied responses\n   - Log the call stack to identify which code path triggers the second invocation\n\n2. **Trace the filter chain**:\n   - Verify whether the header_mutation filter's `encodeHeaders()` is somehow re-triggering route header evaluation\n   - Check if `maybeInitializeRouteConfigs()` in header_mutation filter causes re-evaluation\n\n3. **Test with/without header_mutation filter**:\n   - Disable the header_mutation filter and observe if duplication persists\n   - This will help isolate whether the filter is part of the problem\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\nThe root fix should ensure `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is called exactly once for local replies:\n\n**Option A** (Recommended): Remove the `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call from the filter manager's lambda in `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` for local replies that already have it applied elsewhere.\n\n**Option B**: Add a guard flag to track whether `finalizeResponseHeaders()` has already been called, preventing double invocation.\n\n**Option C**: Ensure the router's local reply lambda calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` itself, and remove it from the filter manager's wrapper to avoid duplication.\n\nThe preferred approach is **Option A** or refactoring to ensure there's a single, clear point where `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is applied for all response types (proxied, local direct response, and local error responses).\n\n## Files to Review\n\n- `source/common/router/router.cc` - Router filter's timeout and error handling\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` - Local reply handling and encode path\n- `source/common/http/utility.cc` - Local reply preparation\n- replies\n\n3. **The Problem in the Router Filter** (`source/common/router/router.cc` lines 1403-1412):\n   - For upstream errors (timeouts, etc.), the router calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply()` with The root cause is that `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is being invoked twice: once in the filter manager's header preparation lambda and again during the encoder filter chain iteration, specifically through the header_mutation filter's interaction with route-level header processing.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe duplicate header processing occurs due to a split code path in Envoy's local reply handling:\n\n1. **Initial Processing** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` lines 1070-1093, 1120-1145):\n   - When `sendLocalReply()` is called, the filter manager constructs an `Utility::EncodeFunctions` lambda that calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` at line 1074/1125\n   - This lambda is passed to `Utility::prepareLocalReply()`, which invokes it to add route-level headers\n\n2. **Filter Chain Processing** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` lines 1244-1310):\n   - After headers are prepared and stored, the `encodeHeaders()` method is called, which iterates through encoder filters starting from index 0\n   - The header_mutation filter (or other filters) may trigger header evaluation again when processing response headers for local replies\n\n3. **The Problem in the Router Filter** (`source/common/router/router.cc` lines 1403-1412):\n   - For upstream errors (timeouts, etc.), the router calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply()` with a lambda\n   - This lambda eventually reaches the filter manager's lambda wrapper, which calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Code References\n\n**Filter Manager's Local Reply Wrapper** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1122-1130`):\n```cpp\nUtility::EncodeFunctions{\n    [this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {\n      if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n        streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, streamInfo());  // FIRST CALL\n      }\n      if (modify_headers) {\n        modify_headers(headers);\n      }\n    },\n```\n\n**Router's Send Local Reply Call** (`source/common/router/router.cc:1403-1412`):\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(\n    code, body,\n    [dropped, Http::Headers::get().EnvoyOverloadedValues.True);\n      }\n      modify_headers_(headers);\n    },\n    absl::nullopt, details);\n```\n\n**Local Reply Preparation** The root cause is that `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is being invoked twice: once in the filter manager's header preparation lambda and again during the encoder filter chain iteration, specifically through the header_mutation filter's interaction with route-level header processing.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe duplicate header processing occurs due to **double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in the local reply code path**:\n\n### For Direct Responses (Redirects):\n\n1. **First Invocation**: Router filter's lambda (`source/common/router/router.cc:501`)\n   - parameter to `sendLocalReply()`\n\n2. **Second Invocation**: Filter manager's wrapper lambda (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1074,1125`)\n   - Filter manager receives `sendLocalReply()` and creates an `Utility::EncodeFunctions` lambda\n   - This wrapper lambda calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` BEFORE calling the passed `modify_headers` callback\n   - Since `direct_response` and `route_entry` are the **same object** for direct responses (see config_impl.cc:1287-1295), `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is invoked twice on the same headers\n\n### Critical Discovery:\n\nIn direct response entry,\n  // or a redirect entry.\n  if (isDirectResponse()) {\n    return this;  // ← DirectResponseEntry IS the RouteEntryImplBase\n  } else {\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n}\n```\n\nThis means for redirects and direct responses:\n- `route->directResponseEntry()` returns the `RouteEntryImplBase` object\n- `route->routeEntry()` returns `nullptr`\n- BUT the filter manager still has a check at line 1073: `if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry())`\n\nHowever, for non-direct-response local replies (timeouts, connection failures), the issue manifests differently through double application of the modify_headers_ callbacks.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Code References\n\n**Filter Manager's Local Reply Wrapper** `response_headers_to_add` configuration\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Trigger**: Upstream request times out or fails\n2. **Router timeout handler**: `Filter::onUpstreamTimeoutAbort()` is invoked\n3. determines execution path\n5. **Prepare local reply**: Calls `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` or `prepareLocalReplyViaFilterChain()`\n6. **Wrap in encode functions**: Creates `Utility::EncodeFunctions` lambda that:\n   - Calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` (LINE 1074/1125 of filter_manager.cc) ← **FIRST CALL**\n   - Calls router's modification lambda (which just modifies attempt count)\n7. **Prepare headers**: `Utility::prepareLocalReply()` invokes the `modify_headers_` callback\n   - This calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()`, applying `response_headers_to_add`\n   - Headers now contain duplicated values\n8. **Encode headers**: `encodeLocalReply()` calls `prepared_local_reply->encode_headers_()`\n9. **Filter manager encode**: `FilterManager::encodeHeaders()` iterates through encoder filters\n10. **Header mutation filter**: If present, `HeaderMutation::encodeHeaders()` is called\n    - This may re-evaluate route configs and potentially re-apply header mutations\n11. **Result**: Response headers contain duplicated values in access logs\n\n## The Role of Header Processing Components\n\n### `HeaderValueOption` Proto Fields (`api/envoy/config/core/v3/`)\n\nThe `HeaderValueOption` message has:\n- **`append_action`**: Enum specifying behavior (OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD, APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD, etc.)\n- **Deprecated `append` field**: BoolValue field for backward compatibility\n  - When `append` is not set, proto defaults apply (affects header merge behavior)\n  - This default behavior can interact poorly with the double-invocation\n\n### Header Parser Processing (`source/common/router/header_parser.cc`)\n\nThe `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()` method:\n- Iterates through all configured headers\n- Applies each header based on its `append_action`\n- The OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD action should replace existing headers, but...\n- When called twice, the second invocation sees headers already added by the first invocation\n- If the header key exists from first call, OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD becomes OVERWRITE, causing... wait, that should still work correctly\n\nThe actual duplication likely occurs because:\n- First `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call adds: `x-custom-trace: abc123`\n- Second call (if it happens) adds another: `x-custom-trace: abc123`\n- The OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD only overwrites if the header already exists from BEFORE the route was applied\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Investigation Steps\n\n1. **Verify the double invocation**:\n   - Add debug logging to `finalizeResponseHeaders()` to track how many times it's called for local replies vs proxied responses\n   - Log the call stack to identify which code path triggers the second invocation\n\n2. **Trace the filter chain**:\n   - Verify whether the header_mutation filter's `encodeHeaders()` is somehow re-triggering route header evaluation\n   - Check if `maybeInitializeRouteConfigs()` in header_mutation filter causes re-evaluation\n\n3. **Test with/without header_mutation filter**:\n   - Disable the header_mutation filter and observe if duplication persists\n   - This will help isolate whether the filter is part of the problem\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\nThe root fix should ensure `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is called exactly once for local replies:\n\n**Option A** (Recommended): Remove the `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call from the filter manager's lambda in `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` for local replies that already have it applied elsewhere.\n\n**Option B**: Add a guard flag to track whether `finalizeResponseHeaders()` has already been called, preventing double invocation.\n\n**Option C**: Ensure the router's local reply lambda calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` itself, and remove it from the filter manager's wrapper to avoid duplication.\n\nThe preferred approach is **Option A** or refactoring to ensure there's a single, clear point where `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is applied for all response types (proxied, local direct response, and local error responses).\n\n## Files to Review\n\n- `source/common/router/router.cc` - Router filter's invocations per response type in metrics\n- Use this to confirm the duplication hypothesis before implementing the fix","originalFile":"# Investigation Report: Duplicate Response Headers in Envoy Filter Pipeline\n\n## Summary\n\nResponse headers configured via `response_headers_to_add` in route configuration are duplicated when the router filter generates local replies (e.g., upstream timeout, connection failure). The root cause is that `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is being invoked twice: once in the filter manager's header preparation lambda and again during the encoder filter chain iteration, specifically through the header_mutation filter's interaction with route-level header processing.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe duplicate header processing occurs due to **double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in the local reply code path**:\n\n### For Direct Responses (Redirects):\n\n1. **First Invocation**: Router filter's lambda (`source/common/router/router.cc:501`)\n   - Router detects direct response and calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply()`\n   - Passes a lambda that calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - This is stored as the `modify_headers` parameter to `sendLocalReply()`\n\n2. **Second Invocation**: Filter manager's wrapper lambda (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1074,1125`)\n   - Filter manager receives `sendLocalReply()` and creates an `Utility::EncodeFunctions` lambda\n   - This wrapper lambda calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` BEFORE calling the passed `modify_headers` callback\n   - Since `direct_response` and `route_entry` are the **same object** for direct responses (see config_impl.cc:1287-1295), `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is invoked twice on the same headers\n\n### Critical Discovery:\n\nIn `source/common/router/config_impl.cc:1287-1295`:\n```cpp\nconst DirectResponseEntry* RouteEntryImplBase::directResponseEntry() const {\n  // A route for a request can exclusively be a route entry, a direct response entry,\n  // or a redirect entry.\n  if (isDirectResponse()) {\n    return this;  // ← DirectResponseEntry IS the RouteEntryImplBase\n  } else {\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n}\n```\n\nThis means for redirects and direct responses:\n- `route->directResponseEntry()` returns the `RouteEntryImplBase` object\n- `route->routeEntry()` returns `nullptr`\n- BUT the filter manager still has a check at line 1073: `if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry())`\n\nHowever, for non-direct-response local replies (timeouts, connection failures), the issue manifests differently through double application of the modify_headers_ callbacks.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Code References\n\n**Filter Manager's Local Reply Wrapper** The root cause is that `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is being invoked twice: once in the filter manager's header preparation lambda and again during the encoder filter chain iteration, specifically and `route_entry` are the **same object** for direct responses (see config_impl.cc:1287-1295), `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is invoked twice on the same headers\n\n### Critical Discovery:\n\nIn }\n}\n```\n\nThis means for redirects and direct responses:\n- `route->directResponseEntry()` returns the `RouteEntryImplBase` object\n- `route->routeEntry()` returns `nullptr`\n- BUT the filter manager still has a check at line 1073: `if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry())`\n\nHowever, for non-direct-response local replies (timeouts, connection failures), the issue Router detects direct response and calls `callbacks_->sendLocalReply()`\n   - Passes a lambda that calls `direct_response->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n   - This is stored as the `modify_headers` parameter to `sendLocalReply()`\n\n2. **Second Invocation**: Filter manager's wrapper lambda (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1074,1125`)\n   - Filter manager receives `sendLocalReply()` and creates an `Utility::EncodeFunctions` lambda\n   - This wrapper lambda calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` BEFORE calling the passed `modify_headers` callback\n   - Since `direct_response` and `route_entry` are the **same object** for direct responses (see config_impl.cc:1287-1295), `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is invoked twice on the same headers\n\n### Critical Discovery:\n\nIn `source/common/router/config_impl.cc:1287-1295`:\n```cpp\nconst DirectResponseEntry* RouteEntryImplBase::directResponseEntry() const {\n  // A route for a request can exclusively be a route entry, a direct response entry,\n  // or a redirect entry.\n  if (isDirectResponse()) {\n    return this;  // ← DirectResponseEntry IS the RouteEntryImplBase\n  } else {\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n}\n```\n\nThis means for redirects and direct responses:\n- `route->directResponseEntry()` returns the `RouteEntryImplBase` object\n- `route->routeEntry()` returns `nullptr`\n- BUT the filter manager still has a check at line 1073: `if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry())`\n\nHowever, for non-direct-response local replies (timeouts, connection failures), the issue manifests differently through double application of the modify_headers_ callbacks.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### Code References\n\n**Filter Manager's Local Reply Wrapper** Specifically:\n\n1. **Filter Manager's Wrapper Lambda** (lines 1074/1125 of `filter_manager.cc`) - Calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` when preparing local replies\n\n2. **Router Filter's Lambda** (line 501 of `router.cc`) - Also calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` for direct responses, and the direct_response object IS the route_entry for redirects\n\n3. **Encoder Filter Chain** - Encoder filters may re-process route configuration, potentially causing duplicate header application\n\n## Key Evidence\n\n- **Code path 1**: `Filter::decodeHeaders()` → `callbacks_->sendLocalReply()` with router's lambda\n- **Code path 2**: `FilterManager::sendLocalReply()` → `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` → Creates wrapper lambda calling `finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n- **Code path 3**: `FilterManager::encodeHeaders()` iterates through encoder filters which may re-evaluate route headers\n\n## Affected Components\n\n- `source/common/router/router.cc` - Router filter's timeout/error handling\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` - Local reply handling and filter chain\n- `source/common/http/utility.cc` - Local reply preparation\n- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_mutation/` - Filter chain interaction\n- `source/common/router/config_impl.cc` - Route entry header finalization\n- Proto definitions with `response_headers_to_add` and `append_action`\n\nThe report includes diagnostic recommendations and three fix options (restructuring header finalization, state tracking, or path separation)."}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1007,"cache_read_input_tokens":114234,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1007},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"753ef650-de05-47c1-87d4-5f1e26181c88","uuid":"6b7eccb9-03d9-4639-8584-0dfa2479beaa"}
